This approach is used for all results where the functional currency is not the U.S. dollar. Accenture&#8217;s management believes that information regarding changes in its revenues and bookings that excludes the effect of fluctuations in foreign currency exchange rates facilitates meaningful comparison of its revenues.</span></div></td></tr></table><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:12px;font-size:10pt;"><span style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;">Reconciliations of these non-GAAP financial measures to the most directly comparable financial measures calculated and presented in accordance with GAAP are included in the news release. full-year revenue growth to 3.5-4.5% in local currency from 3-6% previously, and its range for EPS to </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">NEW YORK; June 25, 2020 &#8212; Accenture (NYSE: ACN) reported financial results for the third quarter of fiscal 2020, ended May 31, 2020, with revenues of $11.0&#160;billion, a decrease of 1% in U.S. dollars and an increase of 1.3% in local currency over the same period last year. Revenue growth for the quarter was reduced approximately 2 percentage points by a decline in revenues from reimbursable travel costs.   </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Diluted earnings per share were $1.90, compared with $1.93 for the third quarter last year.  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Operating income was $1.71 billion, compared with $1.72 billion for the same period last year, and operating margin was 15.6%, an expansion of 10 basis points.  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">New bookings for the quarter were $11.0 billion, with consulting bookings of $6.2&#160;billion and outsourcing bookings of $4.8&#160;billion.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Julie Sweet, Accenture&#8217;s chief executive officer, said, &#8220;In times of crisis, our laser focus on creating value for our clients, our ability to deliver mission-critical services for the world&#8217;s leading companies, and our unwavering commitment to our people and to living our core values inside and outside Accenture make a difference.&#160;I am proud of how we helped ensure the business continuity of our clients, while prioritizing the health and well-being of our people, and continued to deliver on our commitments to our shareholders.&#160;We delivered third-quarter financial results that aligned with our expectations, including revenue growth in the top end of our guided range as well as strong profitability and free cash flow, while continuing to invest in our business and our people.&#8221;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div><br></div><div style="text-align:center;"><div of fiscal 2020 were $11.0&#160;billion, compared with $11.1&#160;billion for the third quarter of fiscal 2019, a decrease of 1% in U.S. dollars and a 1.3% increase in local currency. Revenues for the quarter reflect a foreign-exchange impact of approximately negative 2.5%, compared with the negative 1.5% impact we had previously assumed. Adjusting for the actual foreign-exchange impact, the company&#8217;s guided range for quarterly revenues was approximately $10.65 billion to $11.05&#160;billion. Accenture&#8217;s third quarter fiscal 2020 revenues were in the top end of this adjusted range. &#160;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; The $0.03 decrease in EPS reflects:</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; </font></div></td></tr></table><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;padding-left:24px;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">offset by</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;padding-left:24px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman;  </font></div></td></tr></table><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:48px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:11pt;padding-left:24px;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#9642;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">a $0.02 decrease from higher non-operating expense; and </font></div></td></tr></table><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:48px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:11pt;padding-left:24px;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#9642;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">a $0.01 decrease from higher income attributable to noncontrolling interests. </font></div></td></tr></table><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;padding-left:48px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Gross margin (gross profit as a percentage of revenues) for the quarter was 32.1%, compared with 31.8% for the third quarter last year. Selling, general and administrative (SG&amp;A) expenses for the quarter were $1.82 billion, or 16.5% of revenues, compared with $1.81&#160;billion, or 16.3% of revenues, for the third quarter last year. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Operating income for the quarter was $1.71 billion, or 15.6% of revenues, compared with $1.72&#160;billion, or 15.5% of revenues, for the third quarter of fiscal 2019.  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">The company&#8217;s effective tax rate for the quarter was 25.5%, compared with 25.6% for the third quarter last year. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Net income for the quarter was $1.25 billion, compared with $1.27 billion for the third quarter last year. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Operating cash flow for the quarter was $2.74 billion and property and equipment additions were $150&#160;million. Free cash flow, defined as operating cash flow net of property and equipment additions, was $2.59&#160;billion for the quarter. For the same period last year, operating cash flow was $2.12 billion; property and equipment additions were $140&#160;million; and free cash flow was $1.98 billion. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Days services outstanding, or DSOs, were 41 days at May 31, 2020, compared with 40 days at Aug. 31, 2019 and 39 days at May 31, 2019. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div><br></div><div style="text-align:center;"><div style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Accenture&#8217;s total cash balance at May 31, 2020 was $6.4&#160;billion, compared with $5.4 billion at Feb. 29, 2020 and $6.1&#160;billion at Aug. 31, 2019. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font company has moved from a semi-annual to a quarterly schedule for dividend payments in fiscal 2020. On May 15, 2020, a quarterly cash dividend of $0.80 per share was paid to shareholders of record at the close of business on Apr. 16, 2020. These cash dividend payments totaled $509 million, bringing dividend payments for the year to date to $1.53&#160;billion.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div><br></div><div style="text-align:center;"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><div><br></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Accenture plc has declared another quarterly cash dividend of $0.80 per share for shareholders of record at the close of business on July 16, 2020. This dividend is payable on Aug. 14, 2020. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">In fiscal 2019, the company paid semi-annual cash dividends of $1.46&#160;per share, equivalent to quarterly payments of $0.73 per share. The quarterly dividend of $0.80 per share this year represents a 10% increase over the equivalent quarterly rate in fiscal 2019. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Share Repurchase Activity</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">During the third quarter of fiscal 2020, Accenture repurchased or redeemed 3.7&#160;million shares, including 3.5 million shares repurchased in the open market, for a total of $627&#160;million. This brings Accenture&#8217;s total share repurchases and redemptions for the first three quarters of fiscal 2020 to 12.2 million shares, including 9.5 million shares repurchased in the open market, for a total of $2.33 billion.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">Accenture&#8217;s total remaining share repurchase authority at May 31, 2020 was approximately $1.9&#160;billion.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">At May 31, 2020, Accenture had approximately 637&#160;million total shares outstanding.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline;">Business Outlook</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;">The coronavirus (COVID-19) crisis has created a significant amount of volatility, uncertainty and economic disruption. Accenture&#8217;s fourth-quarter and full-year 2020 business outlook reflects its assumptions, as of today, regarding the continued effect of the coronavirus pandemic. The extent to which this continues to impact Accenture&#8217;s business, operations, and financial results, including the duration and magnitude of such impact, will depend on numerous evolving factors that are difficult to accurately predict, including those discussed in the Risk Factors set forth in Accenture&#8217;s Annual Report on Form 10-K and third-quarter Form 10-Q filings with the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div Pursuant to the requirements of this regulation, reconciliations of this non-GAAP financial information to Accenture&#8217;s financial statements as prepared under generally accepted accounting principles (GAAP) are included in this press release. Financial results &#8220;in local currency&#8221; are calculated by restating current-period activity into U.S. dollars using the comparable prior-year period&#8217;s foreign-currency exchange rates. Accenture&#8217;s management believes providing investors with this information gives additional insights into Accenture&#8217;s results of operations. While Accenture&#8217;s management believes that the non-GAAP financial measures herein are useful in evaluating Accenture&#8217;s operations, this information should be considered as supplemental in nature and not as a substitute for the related financial information prepared in accordance with GAAP. if Accenture is unable to keep its supply of skills and resources in balance with client demand around the world and attract and retain professionals with strong leadership skills, the company&#8217;s business, the utilization rate of the company&#8217;s professionals and the company&#8217;s results of operations may be materially adversely affected; changes in Accenture&#8217;s level of taxes, as well as audits, investigations and tax proceedings, or changes in tax laws or in their interpretation or enforcement, could have a material adverse effect on the company&#8217;s effective tax rate, results of operations, cash flows and financial condition;
